href=\"http://www.paulaschoice.com\" target=\"_blank\">www.PaulasChoice.com</a> and how we collect, use, maintain, protect, and disclose that information.  This policy will apply when you visit www.PaulasChoice.com, www.Beautypedia.com or any other website that links to this policy (each, the \"<strong>Site</strong>\"). </p>\n<p>This policy applies to information we may collect via the Site and via email, text, or other electronic messages between you and us.</p>\n<p>This policy does not apply to information collected when you communicate with us by any other means, including through other websites operated by us or a third party or information about you collected by a third party.</p>\n<p>By accessing or using the Site, you agree to this policy.  If you do not agree with this policy, then you should not access or use the Site.  This policy may change from time to time.  Your continued use of the Site after we make changes constitutes your acceptance of those changes. </p>\n<p><strong><u>INTERNATIONAL USERS</u></strong><br>\n We have legal entities in other countries, including in the EU. The Site is intended for U.S. and Canadian users only. If you are outside the United States or Canada, and you decide to access or use the Site and share your personal information with us, you are consenting to the transfer of your personal information from your current location to the offices and servers of our company and authorized third parties in the United States, and the processing and storage of it by us in the United States. We will process your personal information in accordance with this Privacy Policy.</p>\n<p><strong><u>INFORMATION WE MAY COLLECT ABOUT YOU </u></strong><br>\nWe may collect Personal Information and Non-Personal Information from you when you use the Site:</p>\n<ul>\n  • “<strong>Personal Information</strong>” is information that identifies you personally, which may include your name, mailing address, e-mail address, telephone number, or any other identifier by which you may be contacted online or offline.<br>\n  • “<strong>Non-Personal Information</strong>” is information that does not identify you personally, such as your browser type, your internet connection, your IP address, the URL of the previous web site you visited, the equipment you use to access the Site, and details about how you use the Site. <br>\n</ul>\n<p>This policy refers to Personal Information and Non-Personal Information collectively as “<strong>Information.</strong>”</p>\n<p><strong><u>HOW WE COLLECT YOUR INFORMATION</u></strong></p>\n<p>We may collect Information about you (1) when you provide it to us, and (2) automatically through the Site.</p>\n<p><u>Information You Provide to Us</u><br>\n You may provide us with your Information, including when you:</p>\n<ul>\n  • Visit the Site; <br>\n  • Register or create an account on the Site;<br>\n  • Make a purchase through the Site;<br>\n  • Contact us; or<br>\n  • Submit a product review.<br>\n</ul>\n<p><u>Information We Collect Automatically</u><br>\nWhen you access and use the Site, we may use automatic data collection technologies to automatically collect certain Information about you, including:</p>\n<ul>\n  • Details of your visits to our Site, including traffic data, location data (based on IP address), logs, and other communication data and the resources that you access and use on the Site; or<br>\n  • Information about your computer and internet connection, including your IP address, operating system, and browser type.<br>\n</ul>\n<p>We and our service providers may use some of the following technologies to automatically collect Information about your activities on our Site.</p>\n<p><strong>Cookies</strong><br>\nCookies are small files placed on the hard drive of your computer. You may refuse to accept browser cookies by activating the appropriate setting on your browser. However, if you refuse cookies you may be unable to access certain parts of our Site. Unless you have adjusted your browser setting so that it will refuse cookies, our system will issue cookies when you direct your browser to our Site.</p>\n<p><strong>Flash Cookies</strong><br>\nFlash Cookies (also called local stored objects) collect and store information about your preferences and navigation to, from, and on our Site.</p>\n<p><strong>Web beacons, clear pixels, or pixel tags</strong><br>\nWeb beacons are transparent image files used to monitor your journey around our Site and can help us understand how you interact with our Site.</p>\n<p><strong>Web server logs</strong><br>\nWeb server logs are a historical record of your activity in connection with your use of our Site. For example, a web server log may record the search term you used that directed you to our Site.  It may also collect information about the browser you use when visiting our Site, and other metadata related to your device.</p>\n<p><strong>Geo-location technologies</strong><br>\nGeo-location technologies, including your IP address, may allow us to determine your location.  </p>\n<p>We may also use these technologies to collect Information about your online activities over time and across third-party websites or other online services (behavioral tracking).  </p>\n<p><u>Third Party Partners and Service Providers</u><br>\n Some content, including advertisements, on the Site may be served by third-parties, including advertisers, ad networks and servers, content providers, and application providers. These third parties may use cookies or other tracking technologies to collect information about you when you use our Site. We do not control these third parties' tracking technologies or how they may be used. If you have any questions about an advertisement or other targeted content, you should contact the responsible provider directly.</p>\n<p><u><strong>HOW WE USE YOUR INFORMATION</strong></u><br>\n We may use the Information provided by or collected from you in order to: </p>\n<ul>\n  • Make the Site available to you;<br>\n  • Provide you with information, products, or services;<br>\n  • Fulfill any other purpose for which you provide the Information; <br>\n  • Improve the Site and our business; or<br>\n  • To provide you with notices about your account.<br>\n</ul>\n<p>We may also use this information in any other way we may describe at the time you provide the Information to us, and for any other purpose with your consent.</p>\n<p><strong><u>DISCLOSURE OF YOUR PERSONAL INFORMATION</u></strong><br>\n We may disclose your Personal Information in the following ways:</p>\n<ul>\n  • To fulfill the purpose for which you provide it (for example, if you give us an email address in order to provide you with more information about the Site or our services, we will use that email address to provide the requested information to you, and we may disclose your email address to a service provider performing related services on our behalf, as described below);<br>\n  • To contractors, service providers, and other third-parties we use to support our business, including for such purposes as fulfilling orders, processing credit card payments, delivering packages, sending postal mail and e-mails, providing marketing assistance, analyzing customer data, conducting customer surveys, and providing customer service;<br>\n  • To the general public when you include your Personal Information in your posts or comments on the Site, including, product reviews;<br>\n  • To a buyer or successor in the event of a merger, reorganization, dissolution, or other sale or transfer of some or all of our business or assets;
